msg:After choosing from the Wuta Xinshe series during the May Day holiday, I finally decided to start with the Heniao Hotel. First of all, because the weather in May was still warm and cold, it was too early to go creek tracing, and the hot springs were okay. This hotel just happened not to have a creek in front of the door, and I booked a room with a private hot spring on the balcony. Before checking in, there was a housekeeper and other people to set up a group to provide various useful information. The friends who went to Beibei performed their duties and any questions could be answered in time. The day I arrived was really blue sky and white clouds, coupled with the big ginkgo tree at the door, the mood value was full. There is an infinity pool in the back mountain, but you can't go in the water now, it's beautiful to take pictures. You can also step on bamboo shoots, and the children are very happy. The five meals taste good, and the price is relatively high. There are open-air movies and fireworks at night, and the a**osphere is full. The night of check-in, the "Speeding Life 2" was shown. Although I saw it once in the cinema before, it was still very different to watch it again in an open-air environment. The breakfast is very exquisite. There is a Qingshan Village around the hotel, which is very interesting. It is suitable for going around and walking to the reservoir. There are green waters and green mountains, and the view is particularly good. There is also Heniao Mountain to climb. It's not hot now, so it's nice to go hiking. Suggestion: The sound insulation of the room needs to be improved. In short, if you don't want to go to crowded places or waste time in long queues during holidays, choose a place to relax your eyes, mind and spirit.
